name:L‚Äçe‚Äçi‚Äçc‚Äçe‚Äçs‚Äçt‚Äçe‚Äçr‚Äç ‚ÄçM‚Äça‚Äçn
info:88 Suite
info:Stayed in July 2021
info:Solo travelers
info:56 Reviews
rating:3.2
posted:Posted August 6, 2021
msg:In general, Crowne Plaza Shanghai is a decent hotel. However, from the perspective of a guest, it has several weaknesses that the hotel management may want to pay attention to and work on to continue the legacy of the first Crowne Plaza of the city.

Firstly, the hotel does not have a good location for either business or vacation guests. For business guests, it is too far away from the major business districts of Shanghai. Or, in other words, there are hotels with a standard of amenity, service, and price similar to Crowne Plaza Shanghai but closer to the main business areas. For vacation, the same happens - there are so many similar alternatives closer to the major touristic spots.

Secondly, its hardware is already quite outdated. This puts the hotel in a really disadvantaged position when being compared to competitors mentioned in the first point.

Thirdly, the services guests receive are insufficient. I pick the word "insufficient" instead of "unideal" because the ladies and gentlemen at Crowne Plaza Shanghai are in fact really hard-working, caring, and professional. Their services are great. However, since there are too many guests, no matter how hard the staff work, I can clearly feel that they struggle to let their guests feel their best. Consequently, from the perspective of a guest, the hotel fails to provide the service that Crowne Plaza should be able to offer.

Therefore, I am afraid that Crowne Plaza Shanghai may really be lagging behind its competitors in these three most important regards: location, amenity, and guests' experience.

As a loyal fan of the IHG group, I hope the hotel management could consider working on these issues.
----------------------------------------

The check-in procedure at the front desk was quick, just swipe the room card and take the elevator to the room. The inner and outer rooms are large, suitable for working outside, and have partition doors. Even if you watch TV late at night, it will not affect your rest inside. Breakfast is in the lobby on the first floor. The food and beverages are quite rich, but the layout is a bit awkward. In order to accommodate more people, the layout of the tables is very compact. When there are a lot of people, it is very inconvenient for both those who are sitting and those who are coming out. Overall, as an old five-star hotel, it's pretty good.

msg:I'm not a travel blogger, but I do like staying in good hotels
There are many good hotels in Shanghai, and I want to live in Xujiahui because of poor standards
Boldly tried the Silver Star Crowne Plaza, a pleasant surprise
I was moved by this old five-star restaurant that opened in 1991

When getting off the bus, someone took the initiative to open the door to pick up the luggage
Someone greets you when you enter the door, check-in is smooth
The duty manager helped me take my luggage to the room
Although the facilities in the room are old, but what should be there is not bad
The mouth cup is thin and tall, and the transparent feel is good
People can open the night bed, and there is a small sign to remind you
There are reminder signs everywhere, I'm afraid it's not thoughtful enough
IHG series of pillows are also available, you can choose from 6 types
The bathroom is small, like an old-fashioned five-star hotel
But clean, double shower curtain with bathtub
The high-rise hot water is fast and the water pressure is impressive
The gym is not big, but the equipment is good
Elliptical machine, treadmill, bicycle, yoga room, equipment area, swimming pool
In the afternoon, someone called and arranged for a nucleic acid test at the entrance of the hotel.
I don't need to go out to find it myself, just ask if it's inconvenient or considerate for you!

Because of the itinerary, I have repeatedly entered and exited the hotel many times
Every time I meet service staff and foreign managers at the entrance
English and Chinese take turns to say hello, and don't rush your health code
Do it slowly, do it with you, do it while chatting
Even after working out, go to get supper at nearly 10:00 in the evening
The foreign manager is still in the lobby, chatting with the manager on duty about the World Cup
"What would happen if the Netherlands were first in the group"
Seeing you here, I still greet you warmly, good evening
Meals are also in line with the price, good, there are many choices
It is also appropriate to check out. I asked if you have booked a car.
"Sit and wait for it to cool down outside today"

Some people may ask, isn't this a five-star standard process
But people who live in multiple hotels should know that many new hotels cannot
One detail is easy to do, but every detail is difficult
It is rare for everyone to take good care of guests from the bottom of their hearts
But this old hotel did
What is decent? This is decent!
Not only rely on hardware and Internet celebrities, but also rely on service and experience!
Just let you be taken care of, anyway, I was taken care of well
Some of the more than 1500 people are named here, and no one pulls the door when they arrive,
Stay in a high-end hotel with a 20-minute wait late at night, learn from it!

Not to mention that the hotel belongs to the Shanghai Film Group
The whole is the theme of the movie
Paintings everywhere, movie posters and manuscripts
It's easy to cut, and the accent is also good!

Finally, if you look at the price of Silver Star,
Your jaw will drop in shock, why is it so suitable, you missed it
Don‚Äôt go to live in the new Internet celebrity hotels and fast high-end lines with lower prices
The old five-star sense of detail and decent service cannot be learned, really
I will definitely come back next time I live in Xujiahui. I recommend everyone to try it.
Very sweet! I will come again!
